< Review>
I took over a lease at Copper Beech and lived in the apartment for 2.5 months and paid a total of $1,500 in rent. During my time there, I was rarely in the apartment, never wore shoes inside, never had any guests, and kept things clean and tidy. Upon moving out, I spent about 5-6 hours cleaning and left the place in pristine condition. Copper Beech then charged me $264.66 for general cleaning, carpet cleaning, and painting! Do the math and $264.66 divided by $1,500 comes out to paying 17.6% more than I agreed to pay in rent.

When I tried to voice this concern in person, I was told that the property manager Melanie doesn't take appointments. I sent an email and got a response 14 days later (even though it said in writing that it would take no more than 3 days) saying these charges were just "part of the process [...] of getting the unit ready for the next resident".

Does this sound fair to you?

I have rented in four other places before this and never had any issues. Fresno is a large town and I recommend looking on craigslist or roomies.com for other options that are cheaper and have a sense of honesty. This is my first Google review because I get peeved when individuals are grotesquely unfair.< /Review>

<text>Awesome vegan restaurant that is close to the water - Oceanside pier.  You can order your food inside or call it in.  We happened to go on a Thursday late afternoon before the dinner rush and we had the place to ourselves.

The food is thoughtfully prepared and served with the waiter wearing a mask all of the time. We used the outside dining area which was cozy.  I tried the super veggie burrito and my wife had the YIPPEE-KI-YAY burger with their pretzel bun.  Both items were filling and tasted freshly prepared. It was great to enjoy a completely vegan meal in a kitchen that prepares all plant based meals.

Enjoy eating plants...< /text><user_name>Nasser Salomon< /user_name></record>

< Review>
This place used to be a decent restaurant . It has gone down hill fast. The food is of low quality and it tastes like cardboard. Food tastes like it's been frozen, then defrosted, then frozen again. Definitely it is not fresh food. This place hires illegal immigrants to bus tables, as dish washers, and as chefs, and I've seen them spit in the food. The restrooms are disgusting. I'm surprised the health department hasn't shut this place down. The restrooms are gang graffitied and are always filthy. There are crackheads and homeless people always hanging out in the parking lot. Gang members hang out in this place despite the fact that cops in uniform eat here everyday. People get drunk and out of control at the bar and when there are big sporting events. There is always trash under the tables and old food between the seat cushions in the booths. It takes forever for someone to take your order and forever for them to serve it to you. This place is not worth what they charge for the food and the service they provide. By the way, the fat ugly troll looking piece of trash cop that beat the homeless guy Kelly Thomas to a pulp in Fullerton is frequently seen there stuffing his fat face and talking trash.<//Review>
